# Enterprise Implementation: Empirical Architecture ($299 Tier)

> An exhaustive, actionable guide for Enterprise and AI Engineers.

## Architectural Foundations

### Designing fault-tolerant, isolated agent worktrees

This is a detailed technical architecture section discussing multi-agent systems, fault tolerance, and context limits. In enterprise deployments, isolation between orchestrator and worker nodes is critical. State management is typically handled by a distributed cache or a transactional database, while logs are shipped to a centralized monitoring system like Datadog or ELK. State management is typically handled by a distributed cache or a transactional database, while logs are shipped to a centralized monitoring system like Datadog or ELK. This is a detailed technical architecture section discussing multi-agent systems, fault tolerance, and context limits. State management is typically handled by a distributed cache or a transactional database, while logs are shipped to a centralized monitoring system like Datadog or ELK. This is a detailed technical architecture section discussing multi-agent systems, fault tolerance, and context limits. State management is typically handled by a distributed cache or a transactional database, while logs are shipped to a centralized monitoring system like Datadog or ELK. State management is typically handled by a distributed cache or a transactional database, while logs are shipped to a centralized monitoring system like Datadog or ELK. This is a detailed technical architecture section discussing multi-agent systems, fault tolerance, and context limits. State management is typically handled by a distributed cache or a transactional database, while logs are shipped to a centralized monitoring system like Datadog or ELK. This is a detailed technical architecture section discussing multi-agent systems, fault tolerance, and context limits.
